<h1 class="firstHeading mw-first-heading" id="firstHeading"><span class="mw-page-title-main">卫生设施</span></h1>
<div class="vector-body" id="bodyContent">
<div class="noprint" id="siteSub">维基百科，自由的百科全书</div>
<div id="contentSub"></div>
<div id="contentSub2"></div>
<div id="jump-to-nav"></div>
<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#mw-head">跳到导航</a>
<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#searchInput">跳到搜索</a>
<div class="mw-body-content mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr" id="mw-content-text" lang="zh"><div class="mw-parser-output"><div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Sanitation_Value_Chain.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="750" data-file-width="2300" decoding="async" height="72" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/74/Sanitation_Value_Chain.jpg/220px-Sanitation_Value_Chain.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/74/Sanitation_Value_Chain.jpg/330px-Sanitation_Value_Chain.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/74/Sanitation_Value_Chain.jpg/440px-Sanitation_Value_Chain.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Sanitation_Value_Chain.jpg" title="放大"></a></div>卫生设施系统：收集、运输、处理、处置或<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Reuse of excreta" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="粪便再利用"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%B2%AA%E4%BE%BF%E5%86%8D%E5%88%A9%E7%94%A8&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="粪便再利用（页面不存在）">再利用</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Reuse_of_excreta" title="en:Reuse of excreta"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Reuse of excreta</span></a></span>）</span></span>。</div></div></div>
<p><b>卫生设施</b>，是指涉及<a href="/wiki/%E5%85%AC%E5%85%B1%E5%8D%AB%E7%94%9F" title="公共卫生">公共卫生</a>及<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Environmental health" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="环境卫生"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%8E%AF%E5%A2%83%E5%8D%AB%E7%94%9F&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="环境卫生（页面不存在）">环境卫生</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Environmental_health" title="en:Environmental health"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Environmental health</span></a></span>）</span></span>的设施，包括净化<a href="/wiki/%E9%A5%AE%E7%94%A8%E6%B0%B4" title="饮用水">饮用水</a>和对<a href="/wiki/%E6%8E%92%E6%B3%84%E7%89%A9" title="排泄物">人类粪便</a>进行适当处理和处置，也包括<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Sewage" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="排污"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%8E%92%E6%B1%A1&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="排污（页面不存在）">排污</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sewage" title="en:Sewage"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Sewage</span></a></span>）</span></span>。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-1"><a href="#cite_note-1">[1]</a></sup><a href="/wiki/%E9%A3%8E%E9%99%A9%E7%AE%A1%E7%90%86" title="风险管理">避免</a>人与<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%B2%AA%E4%BE%BF" title="粪便">粪便</a>接触是卫生设施的主要功能，比如用肥皂<a href="/wiki/%E6%B4%97%E6%89%8B" title="洗手">洗手</a>。卫生设施的目的是，通过提供清洁的环境，来保护人类健康。它能阻止<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Transmission (medicine)" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="疾病传播"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%96%BE%E7%97%85%E4%BC%A0%E6%92%AD&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="疾病传播（页面不存在）">疾病传播</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Transmission_(medicine)" title="en:Transmission (medicine)"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Transmission (medicine)</span></a></span>）</span></span>，尤其是通过<a href="/wiki/%E7%B2%AA%E5%8F%A3%E8%B7%AF%E5%BE%84" title="粪口路径">粪口路径</a>。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-:2_2-0"><a href="#cite_note-:2-2">[2]</a></sup>例如，<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%85%B9%E6%B3%BB" title="腹泻">腹泻</a>是导致<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Malnutrition in children" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="儿童营养不良"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%84%BF%E7%AB%A5%E8%90%A5%E5%85%BB%E4%B8%8D%E8%89%AF&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="儿童营养不良（页面不存在）">儿童营养不良</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Malnutrition_in_children" title="en:Malnutrition in children"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Malnutrition in children</span></a></span>）</span></span>和<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Stunted growth" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="发育迟缓"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%8F%91%E8%82%B2%E8%BF%9F%E7%BC%93&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="发育迟缓（页面不存在）">发育迟缓</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Stunted_growth" title="en:Stunted growth"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Stunted growth</span></a></span>）</span></span>的主要原因，可以通过卫生设施来降低它的发生几率。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-3"><a href="#cite_note-3">[3]</a></sup>此外还有许多疾病容易在卫生设施条件较差的社区传播，例如<a href="/wiki/%E8%9B%94%E8%99%AB%E7%97%85" title="蛔虫病">蛔虫病</a>（一种<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Helminthiasis" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="肠道寄生虫病"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%85%B8%E9%81%93%E5%AF%84%E7%94%9F%E8%9F%B2%E7%97%85" title="腸道寄生蟲病">肠道寄生虫病</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Helminthiasis" title="en:Helminthiasis"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Helminthiasis</span></a></span>）</span></span>）、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%9C%8D%E4%B9%B1" title="霍乱">霍乱</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E8%82%9D%E7%82%8E" title="肝炎">肝炎</a>、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%B0%8F%E5%84%BF%E9%BA%BB%E7%97%B9" title="小儿麻痹">小儿麻痹</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E8%A1%80%E5%90%B8%E8%99%AB%E7%97%85" title="血吸虫病">血吸虫病</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E6%B2%99%E7%9C%BC" title="沙眼">沙眼</a>等，这只是其中几个例子。
</p><p>存在一系列的卫生技术和方法，例如：<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Community-led total sanitation" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="社区主导的全面卫生"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%A4%BE%E5%8C%BA%E4%B8%BB%E5%AF%BC%E7%9A%84%E5%85%A8%E9%9D%A2%E5%8D%AB%E7%94%9F&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="社区主导的全面卫生（页面不存在）">社区主导的全面卫生</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Community-led_total_sanitation" title="en:Community-led total sanitation"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Community-led total sanitation</span></a></span>）</span></span>、<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Container-based sanitation" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="基于容器的卫生设施"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9F%BA%E4%BA%8E%E5%AE%B9%E5%99%A8%E7%9A%84%E5%8D%AB%E7%94%9F%E8%AE%BE%E6%96%BD&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="基于容器的卫生设施（页面不存在）">基于容器的卫生设施</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Container-based_sanitation" title="en:Container-based sanitation"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Container-based sanitation</span></a></span>）</span></span>、<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Ecological sanitation" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="生态卫生设施"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%94%9F%E6%80%81%E5%8D%AB%E7%94%9F%E8%AE%BE%E6%96%BD&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="生态卫生设施（页面不存在）">生态卫生设施</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ecological_sanitation" title="en:Ecological sanitation"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Ecological sanitation</span></a></span>）</span></span>、<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Emergency sanitation" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="应急卫生设施"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%BA%94%E6%80%A5%E5%8D%AB%E7%94%9F%E8%AE%BE%E6%96%BD&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="应急卫生设施（页面不存在）">应急卫生设施</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Emergency_sanitation" title="en:Emergency sanitation"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Emergency sanitation</span></a></span>）</span></span>、环境卫生设施、现场卫生设施和<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Sustainable sanitation" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="可持续卫生设施"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%8F%AF%E6%8C%81%E7%BB%AD%E5%8D%AB%E7%94%9F%E8%AE%BE%E6%96%BD&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="可持续卫生设施（页面不存在）">可持续卫生设施</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sustainable_sanitation" title="en:Sustainable sanitation"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Sustainable sanitation</span></a></span>）</span></span>。卫生设施包括对人类排泄物和废水的接纳、存储、运输、处理，以及处置或<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Reuse of human waste" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="人类废物再利用"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%BA%BA%E7%B1%BB%E5%BA%9F%E7%89%A9%E5%86%8D%E5%88%A9%E7%94%A8&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="人类废物再利用（页面不存在）">再利用</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Reuse_of_human_waste" title="en:Reuse of human waste"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Reuse of human waste</span></a></span>）</span></span>。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-4"><a href="#cite_note-4">[4]</a></sup>卫生设施系统内的再利用活动，可能集中于粪便和废水中所含的营养、水、能量或有机物。这些被称为“卫生设施价值链”或“卫生设施经济”。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-5"><a href="#cite_note-5">[5]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-6"><a href="#cite_note-6">[6]</a></sup>
</p><p>为在国家内部或国家间比较服务水平，卫生设施被划分为几个“等级”。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Sanitation_{{!}}_JMP_7-0"><a href="#cite_note-Sanitation_{{!}}_JMP-7">[7]</a></sup><span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Joint Monitoring Programme for Water Supply and Sanitation" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="供水与卫生设施联合监测计划"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%BE%9B%E6%B0%B4%E4%B8%8E%E5%8D%AB%E7%94%9F%E8%AE%BE%E6%96%BD%E8%81%94%E5%90%88%E7%9B%91%E6%B5%8B%E8%AE%A1%E5%88%92&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="供水与卫生设施联合监测计划（页面不存在）">联合监测计划</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Joint_Monitoring_Programme_for_Water_Supply_and_Sanitation" title="en:Joint Monitoring Programme for Water Supply and Sanitation"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Joint Monitoring Programme for Water Supply and Sanitation</span></a></span>）</span></span>（Joint Monitoring Programme，简称JMP）在2016年定义的卫生等级从<a href="/wiki/%E9%9C%B2%E5%A4%A9%E6%8E%92%E4%BE%BF" title="露天排便">露天排便</a>开始，使用“未改进”、“有限”、“基本”等术语逐级升高，一直到最高等级“<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Improved sanitation" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="改善的卫生设施"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%94%B9%E5%96%84%E7%9A%84%E5%8D%AB%E7%94%9F%E8%AE%BE%E6%96%BD&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="改善的卫生设施（页面不存在）">安全管理</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Improved_sanitation" title="en:Improved sanitation"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Improved sanitation</span></a></span>）</span></span>”。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Sanitation_{{!}}_JMP_7-1"><a href="#cite_note-Sanitation_{{!}}_JMP-7">[7]</a></sup>这特别适合<a href="/wiki/%E5%8F%91%E5%B1%95%E4%B8%AD%E5%9B%BD%E5%AE%B6" title="发展中国家">发展中国家</a>。
</p><p><a href="/wiki/%E4%BA%AB%E6%9C%89%E9%A5%AE%E6%B0%B4%E5%92%8C%E5%8D%AB%E7%94%9F%E8%AE%BE%E6%96%BD%E7%9A%84%E4%BA%BA%E6%9D%83" title="享有饮水和卫生设施的人权">享有饮水和卫生设施的人权</a>在2010年得到<a href="/wiki/%E8%81%94%E5%90%88%E5%9B%BD%E5%A4%A7%E4%BC%9A" title="联合国大会">联合国大会</a>的认可。卫生设施是<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%85%A8%E7%90%83%E5%8F%91%E5%B1%95" title="全球发展">全球发展</a>的优先重点，也是<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Sustainable Development Goal 6" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="可持续发展目标6"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%8F%AF%E6%8C%81%E7%BB%AD%E5%8F%91%E5%B1%95%E7%9B%AE%E6%A0%876&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="可持续发展目标6（页面不存在）">可持续发展目标6</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sustainable_Development_Goal_6" title="en:Sustainable Development Goal 6"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Sustainable Development Goal 6</span></a></span>）</span></span>的主题。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-JMP2017_8-0"><a href="#cite_note-JMP2017-8">[8]</a></sup>JMP在2017年的估算表明，目前有45亿人没有安全管理的卫生设施。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-JMP2017_8-1"><a href="#cite_note-JMP2017-8">[8]</a></sup>缺乏卫生设施不仅会影响<a href="/wiki/%E5%85%AC%E5%85%B1%E5%8D%AB%E7%94%9F" title="公共卫生">公共卫生</a>，还会影响人的<a href="/wiki/%E5%B0%8A%E4%B8%A5" title="尊严">尊严</a>和人身安全。
</p>

<h2><span id=".E5.AE.9A.E4.B9.89"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="定义">定义</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%8D%AB%E7%94%9F%E8%AE%BE%E6%96%BD&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="编辑章节：定义">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

codecs="vp8, vorbis"'/></video> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:2011_07-Internal_ReinventTheToilet_Animation.webm" title="放大"></a></div>此动画视频强调了<a href="/wiki/%E5%8F%91%E5%B1%95%E4%B8%AD%E5%9B%BD%E5%AE%B6" title="发展中国家">发展中国家</a><a href="/wiki/%E5%85%AC%E5%85%B1%E5%8D%AB%E7%94%9F" title="公共卫生">公共卫生</a>中卫生设施的重要性（以<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%A9%AC%E6%A1%B6" title="马桶">马桶</a>为例）</div></div></div>
<p><a href="/wiki/%E4%B8%96%E7%95%8C%E5%8D%AB%E7%94%9F%E7%BB%84%E7%BB%87" title="世界卫生组织">世界卫生组织</a>定义的“卫生设施”一词如下：
</p>
<style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r61209892">.mw-parser-output .templatequote{margin-top:0;overflow:hidden}.mw-parser-output .templatequote .templatequotecite{line-height:1em;text-align:left;padding-left:2em;margin-top:0}.mw-parser-output .templatequote .templatequotecite cite{font-size:small}</style>
<blockquote class="templatequote"><p>卫生一般系指提供用于安全处置人类粪便的设施和服务。缺乏环境卫生是全世界一大疾病起因，而改善环境卫生对家庭和整个社区的卫生具有已被确认的显著有益影响。卫生也涉及通过垃圾收集和废水处理等服务保持清洁的环境。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-9"><a href="#cite_note-9">[9]</a></sup></p></blockquote><p> （<a class="external text" href="//web.archive.org/web/20201019030819/http://www.who.int/topics/sanitation/zh/" rel="nofollow">页面存档备份</a>，存于<a href="/wiki/%E4%BA%92%E8%81%94%E7%BD%91%E6%A1%A3%E6%A1%88%E9%A6%86" title="互联网档案馆">互联网档案馆</a>）
</p><p>卫生设施涵盖了以下四类工程基础设施项目（虽然通常只有第一个是与“卫生设施”一词密切相关的）：排泄物管理系统、污水管理系统（这里包括<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%B1%A1%E6%B0%B4%E5%A4%84%E7%90%86" title="污水处理">污水处理</a>）、固体废物管理系统、雨排系统。
</p>
<h2><span id=".E7.9B.AE.E6.A0.87"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="目标">目标</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%8D%AB%E7%94%9F%E8%AE%BE%E6%96%BD&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="编辑章节：目标">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>卫生设施的总体目标是，为每一个人提供健康的生活环境，保护自然资源（例如<a href="/wiki/%E5%9C%B0%E8%A1%A8%E6%B0%B4" title="地表水">地表水</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E5%9C%B0%E4%B8%8B%E6%B0%B4" title="地下水">地下水</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E5%9C%9F%E5%A3%A4" title="土壤">土壤</a>），并在人们<a href="/wiki/%E6%8E%92%E4%BE%BF" title="排便">大便</a>或<a href="/wiki/%E6%8E%92%E5%B0%BF" title="排尿">小便</a>时提供安全和<a href="/wiki/%E5%B0%8A%E4%B8%A5" title="尊严">尊严</a>。
</p><p>我们还有一项<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Human right to water and sanitation" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="人类饮水及卫生设施权力"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%BA%BA%E7%B1%BB%E9%A5%AE%E6%B0%B4%E5%8F%8A%E5%8D%AB%E7%94%9F%E8%AE%BE%E6%96%BD%E6%9D%83%E5%8A%9B&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="人类饮水及卫生设施权力（页面不存在）">关于卫生设施的人权</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Human_right_to_water_and_sanitation" title="en:Human right to water and sanitation"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Human right to water and sanitation</span></a></span>）</span></span>：2010年9月，<a href="/wiki/%E8%81%94%E5%90%88%E5%9B%BD%E4%BA%BA%E6%9D%83%E7%90%86%E4%BA%8B%E4%BC%9A" title="联合国人权理事会">联合国人权理事会</a>通过了一项决议，承认人类对饮水和卫生设施的权力，是适足生活水准下<a href="/wiki/%E4%BA%BA%E6%9D%83" title="人权">人权</a>的一部分。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-10"><a href="#cite_note-10">[10]</a></sup>
</p><p>有效的卫生设施系统形成了排泄物和人类之间的屏障，以这种方式阻断了疾病的<a href="/wiki/%E4%BC%A0%E6%92%AD%E9%80%94%E5%BE%84" title="传播途径">传播途径</a>（例如，在粪便传播疾病的情况下）。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-11"><a href="#cite_note-11">[11]</a></sup>F图具象化了这一方面，其中<a href="/wiki/%E7%B2%AA%E5%8F%A3%E8%B7%AF%E5%BE%84" title="粪口路径">粪口路径</a>中所有的主要途径均以字母F开头：粪便（Feces）、手指（Fingers）、苍蝇（Flies）、田野（Fields）、液体（Fluids）、食物（Food）。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-12"><a href="#cite_note-12">[12]</a></sup>
</p><p>面临的主要挑战之一是提供<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Sustainable sanitation" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="可持续卫生设施"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%8F%AF%E6%8C%81%E7%BB%AD%E5%8D%AB%E7%94%9F%E8%AE%BE%E6%96%BD&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="可持续卫生设施（页面不存在）">可持续卫生设施</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sustainable_sanitation" title="en:Sustainable sanitation"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Sustainable sanitation</span></a></span>）</span></span>，尤其是在<a href="/wiki/%E5%8F%91%E5%B1%95%E4%B8%AD%E5%9B%BD%E5%AE%B6" title="发展中国家">发展中国家</a>。持续维持卫生设施具有技术、制度和社会等方面的性质。卫生基础设施必须适应多种特定情况，包括消费者的期望和当地可用的资源。
</p><p>卫生设施技术可能涉及集中化的<a href="/wiki/%E5%9C%9F%E6%9C%A8%E5%B7%A5%E7%A8%8B" title="土木工程">土木工程</a>结构，例如<a href="/wiki/%E4%B8%8B%E6%B0%B4%E9%81%93" title="下水道">下水道</a>、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%B1%A1%E6%B0%B4%E5%A4%84%E7%90%86" title="污水处理">污水处理</a>、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%9C%B0%E8%A1%A8%E5%BE%84%E6%B5%81" title="地表径流">地表径流</a>处理和固体废物<a href="/wiki/%E5%A0%86%E5%A1%AB" title="堆填">掩埋</a>。这些结构被设计用来处理<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%BA%9F%E6%B0%B4" title="废水">废水</a>和<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%9F%8E%E5%B8%82%E5%9B%BA%E4%BD%93%E5%BA%9F%E7%89%A9" title="城市固体废物">城市固体废物</a>。卫生设施技术也可以采取相对简单的现场卫生设施系统的形式。在某些情况下，可以采取简易<a href="/wiki/%E6%97%B1%E5%BB%81" title="旱廁">旱厕</a>的形式，或其它类型的用于<a href="/wiki/%E6%8E%92%E6%B3%84%E7%89%A9" title="排泄物">排泄物</a>管理的<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Dry toilet" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="免冲水马桶"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%85%8D%E5%86%B2%E6%B0%B4%E9%A9%AC%E6%A1%B6&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="免冲水马桶（页面不存在）">免冲水马桶</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dry_toilet" title="en:Dry toilet"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Dry toilet</span></a></span>）</span></span>。
</p><p>为人们提供卫生设施需要关注整个系统，而不仅仅是关注技术方面，比如<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%A9%AC%E6%A1%B6" title="马桶">马桶</a>、<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Fecal sludge management" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="粪便污泥管理"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%B2%AA%E4%BE%BF%E6%B1%A1%E6%B3%A5%E7%AE%A1%E7%90%86&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="粪便污泥管理（页面不存在）">粪便污泥管理</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fecal_sludge_management" title="en:Fecal sludge management"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Fecal sludge management</span></a></span>）</span></span>或<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%B1%A1%E6%B0%B4%E5%A4%84%E7%90%86%E5%8E%82" title="污水处理厂">污水处理厂</a>。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Tilley_13-0"><a href="#cite_note-Tilley-13">[13]</a></sup>“卫生链”涉及到用户习惯、粪便和废水的收集方法、废物运输及处理，以及再利用或处置。所有这些都需要通盘考虑。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Tilley_13-1"><a href="#cite_note-Tilley-13">[13]</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span id=".E7.B1.BB.E5.9E.8B.E5.92.8C.E6.9C.AF.E8.AF.AD"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="类型和术语">类型和术语</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%8D%AB%E7%94%9F%E8%AE%BE%E6%96%BD&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="编辑章节：类型和术语">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Percentage_of_population_served_by_different_types_of_sanitation_systems.png"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="535" data-file-width="780" decoding="async" height="151" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/de/Percentage_of_population_served_by_different_types_of_sanitation_systems.png/220px-Percentage_of_population_served_by_different_types_of_sanitation_systems.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/de/Percentage_of_population_served_by_different_types_of_sanitation_systems.png/330px-Percentage_of_population_served_by_different_types_of_sanitation_systems.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/de/Percentage_of_population_served_by_different_types_of_sanitation_systems.png/440px-Percentage_of_population_served_by_different_types_of_sanitation_systems.png 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Percentage_of_population_served_by_different_types_of_sanitation_systems.png" title="放大"></a></div>不同类型的卫生设施系统所服务人口的百分比<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-14"><a href="#cite_note-14">[14]</a></sup></div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Shower,_double-vault_urine-diverting_dry_toilet_(UDDT)_and_waterless_urinal_in_Lima,_Peru.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1200" data-file-width="1600" decoding="async" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0d/Shower%2C_double-vault_urine-diverting_dry_toilet_%28UDDT%29_and_waterless_urinal_in_Lima%2C_Peru.jpg/220px-Shower%2C_double-vault_urine-diverting_dry_toilet_%28UDDT%29_and_waterless_urinal_in_Lima%2C_Peru.jpg" title="放大"></a></div>卫生基础设施的示例：秘鲁<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%88%A9%E9%A9%AC" title="利马">利马</a>的淋浴、双位<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Urine-diverting dry toilet" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="粪尿分离干厕"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%B2%AA%E5%B0%BF%E5%88%86%E7%A6%BB%E5%B9%B2%E5%8E%95&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="粪尿分离干厕（页面不存在）">粪尿分离干厕</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Urine-diverting_dry_toilet" title="en:Urine-diverting dry toilet"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Urine-diverting dry toilet</span></a></span>）</span></span>（UDDT）和无水<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%B0%8F%E4%BE%BF%E5%99%A8" title="小便器">小便器</a></div></div></div>
<p>卫生设施一词加上不同的限定语或形容词，就能表示不同类型的卫生设施系统（可能仅涉及人类<a href="/wiki/%E6%8E%92%E6%B3%84%E7%89%A9" title="排泄物">排泄物</a>管理或涉及整个卫生系统，即同时涉及灰水、雨水和固体废物管理）-按对应英文的字母顺序：
</p>
<h3><span id=".E5.9F.BA.E6.9C.AC.EF.BC.88Basic.EF.BC.89.E5.8D.AB.E7.94.9F.E8.AE.BE.E6.96.BD"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="基本（Basic）卫生设施">基本（Basic）卫生设施</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%8D%AB%E7%94%9F%E8%AE%BE%E6%96%BD&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="编辑章节：基本（Basic）卫生设施">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>2017年，<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Joint Monitoring Programme for Water Supply and Sanitation" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="供水与卫生设施联合监测计划"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%BE%9B%E6%B0%B4%E4%B8%8E%E5%8D%AB%E7%94%9F%E8%AE%BE%E6%96%BD%E8%81%94%E5%90%88%E7%9B%91%E6%B5%8B%E8%AE%A1%E5%88%92&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="供水与卫生设施联合监测计划（页面不存在）">JMP</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Joint_Monitoring_Programme_for_Water_Supply_and_Sanitation" title="en:Joint Monitoring Programme for Water Supply and Sanitation"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Joint Monitoring Programme for Water Supply and Sanitation</span></a></span>）</span></span>定义了一个新的术语：“基本卫生设施服务”。它被定义为不与其它家庭共用的<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Improved sanitation" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="改善的卫生设施"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%94%B9%E5%96%84%E7%9A%84%E5%8D%AB%E7%94%9F%E8%AE%BE%E6%96%BD&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="改善的卫生设施（页面不存在）">改善的卫生设施</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Improved_sanitation" title="en:Improved sanitation"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Improved sanitation</span></a></span>）</span></span>。较低水平的服务现在被称为“有限的卫生设施服务”，指的是两个家庭或更多家庭之间共用的改善的卫生设施。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-JMP2017_8-2"><a href="#cite_note-JMP2017-8">[8]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id=".E5.9F.BA.E4.BA.8E.E5.AE.B9.E5.99.A8.E7.9A.84.EF.BC.88Container-based.EF.BC.89.E5.8D.AB.E7.94.9F.E8.AE.BE.E6.96.BD"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="基于容器的（Container-based）卫生设施">基于容器的（Container-based）卫生设施</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%8D%AB%E7%94%9F%E8%AE%BE%E6%96%BD&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="编辑章节：基于容器的（Container-based）卫生设施">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Container-based sanitation" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="基于容器的卫生设施"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9F%BA%E4%BA%8E%E5%AE%B9%E5%99%A8%E7%9A%84%E5%8D%AB%E7%94%9F%E8%AE%BE%E6%96%BD&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="基于容器的卫生设施（页面不存在）">基于容器的卫生设施</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Container-based_sanitation" title="en:Container-based sanitation"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Container-based sanitation</span></a></span>）</span></span>（CBS）是指人类<a href="/wiki/%E6%8E%92%E6%B3%84%E7%89%A9" title="排泄物">排泄物</a>被收集在可密封、可移动的容器中，然后被运输到处理设施。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Tilmans_15-0"><a href="#cite_note-Tilmans-15">[15]</a></sup>基于容器的卫生设施通常作为一项服务提供，涉及提供某些类型的<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Portable toilet" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="可移动厕所"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%8F%AF%E7%A7%BB%E5%8A%A8%E5%8E%95%E6%89%80&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="可移动厕所（页面不存在）">可移动厕所</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Portable_toilet" title="en:Portable toilet"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Portable toilet</span></a></span>）</span></span>，并收集排泄物，费用由用户承担。通过适当地发展、支持和运作伙伴关系，CBS可以为低收入城市人口提供安全的粪便收集、运输和处理服务，而其成本比安装和维护<a href="/wiki/%E4%B8%8B%E6%B0%B4%E9%81%93" title="下水道">下水道</a>的成本低。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Shepardj_16-0"><a href="#cite_note-Shepardj-16">[16]</a></sup>在大多数情况下，CBS是基于<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Urine-diverting dry toilet" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="尿便分离旱厕"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%B0%BF%E4%BE%BF%E5%88%86%E7%A6%BB%E6%97%B1%E5%8E%95&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="尿便分离旱厕（页面不存在）">尿便分离旱厕</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Urine-diverting_dry_toilet" title="en:Urine-diverting dry toilet"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Urine-diverting dry toilet</span></a></span>）</span></span>的使用的。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E7.A4.BE.E5.8C.BA.E4.B8.BB.E5.AF.BC.E7.9A.84.EF.BC.88Community-led.EF.BC.89.E5.85.A8.E9.9D.A2.E5.8D.AB.E7.94.9F.E8.AE.BE.E6.96.BD"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="社区主导的（Community-led）全面卫生设施">社区主导的（Community-led）全面卫生设施</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%8D%AB%E7%94%9F%E8%AE%BE%E6%96%BD&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="编辑章节：社区主导的（Community-led）全面卫生设施">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Community-led total sanitation" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="社区主导的全面卫生设施"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%A4%BE%E5%8C%BA%E4%B8%BB%E5%AF%BC%E7%9A%84%E5%85%A8%E9%9D%A2%E5%8D%AB%E7%94%9F%E8%AE%BE%E6%96%BD&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="社区主导的全面卫生设施（页面不存在）">社区主导的全面卫生设施</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Community-led_total_sanitation" title="en:Community-led total sanitation"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Community-led total sanitation</span></a></span>）</span></span>（CLTS）是一种主要在农村人口中，通过“触发”过程，实现<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Behavior change (public health" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="行为养成 (公共卫生)"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%BA%E5%85%BB%E6%88%90_(%E5%85%AC%E5%85%B1%E5%8D%AB%E7%94%9F)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="行为养成 (公共卫生)（页面不存在）">行为养成)</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Behavior_change_(public_health" title="en:Behavior change (public health"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Behavior change (public health</span></a></span>）</span></span>的方法，目的是促进自发且长期放弃<a href="/wiki/%E9%9C%B2%E5%A4%A9%E6%8E%92%E4%BE%BF" title="露天排便">露天排便</a>的做法。CLTS采用一种使农村卫生设施无需补充硬件设施即可工作的方法，促使社区认识到露天排便的问题，并通过<a href="/wiki/%E9%9B%86%E4%BD%93%E8%A1%8C%E5%8A%A8" title="集体行动">集体行动</a>来“消灭露天排便”。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E5.B9.B2.E5.BC.8F.EF.BC.88Dry.EF.BC.89.E5.8D.AB.E7.94.9F.E8.AE.BE.E6.96.BD"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="干式（Dry）卫生设施">干式（Dry）卫生设施</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%8D%AB%E7%94%9F%E8%AE%BE%E6%96%BD&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="编辑章节：干式（Dry）卫生设施">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>“干式卫生设施”一词并没有被广泛使用，也没有非常明确的定义。它通常是指采用某种<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Dry toilet" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="旱厕"><span class="ilh-page"><a href="/wiki/%E6%97%B1%E5%BB%81" title="旱廁">旱厕</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dry_toilet" title="en:Dry toilet"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Dry toilet</span></a></span>）</span></span>且没有下水道来排走粪便的系统。通常人们所谓的“干式卫生设施”，意思是一个采用<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Urine-diverting dry toilet" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="尿便分离旱厕"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%B0%BF%E4%BE%BF%E5%88%86%E7%A6%BB%E6%97%B1%E5%8E%95&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="尿便分离旱厕（页面不存在）">尿便分离旱厕</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Urine-diverting_dry_toilet" title="en:Urine-diverting dry toilet"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Urine-diverting dry toilet</span></a></span>）</span></span>（UDDT）的卫生设施系统。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-17"><a href="#cite_note-17">[17]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Platzer_18-0"><a href="#cite_note-Platzer-18">[18]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Flores_19-0"><a href="#cite_note-Flores-19">[19]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id=".E7.94.9F.E6.80.81.EF.BC.88Ecological.EF.BC.89.E5.8D.AB.E7.94.9F.E8.AE.BE.E6.96.BD"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="生态（Ecological）卫生设施">生态（Ecological）卫生设施</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%8D%AB%E7%94%9F%E8%AE%BE%E6%96%BD&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="编辑章节：生态（Ecological）卫生设施">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Ecological sanitation" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="生态卫生设施"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%94%9F%E6%80%81%E5%8D%AB%E7%94%9F%E8%AE%BE%E6%96%BD&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="生态卫生设施（页面不存在）">生态卫生设施</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ecological_sanitation" title="en:Ecological sanitation"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Ecological sanitation</span></a></span>）</span></span>是一种方法，而不是一种技术或设备，其特征是希望以安全的方式在卫生设施和农业之间建立“闭环”（主要是养分和有机物） 。换句话说：“生态卫生设施系统将粪便资源（植物养分和有机物）安全地循环利用到作物生产中，从而最大限度地减少不可再生资源的使用”。通过适当的设计和操作，生态卫生设施系统可提供卫生安全、经济且闭环的系统，以将人类排泄物转化为养分返回到土壤，将水返回到地面。生态卫生也被称为资源导向的卫生设施。<sup class="noprint Template-Fact"><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:%E5%88%97%E6%98%8E%E6%9D%A5%E6%BA%90" title="Wikipedia:列明来源"><span style="white-space: nowrap;" title="来源请求。">[來源請求]</span></a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Emergency_pit_lining_kits_by_Evenproducts_(6619616945).jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1200" data-file-width="1600" decoding="async" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/68/Emergency_pit_lining_kits_by_Evenproducts_%286619616945%29.jpg/220px-Emergency_pit_lining_kits_by_Evenproducts_%286619616945%29.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/68/Emergency_pit_lining_kits_by_Evenproducts_%286619616945%29.jpg/330px-Emergency_pit_lining_kits_by_Evenproducts_%286619616945%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/68/Emergency_pit_lining_kits_by_Evenproducts_%286619616945%29.jpg/440px-Emergency_pit_lining_kits_by_Evenproducts_%286619616945%29.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Emergency_pit_lining_kits_by_Evenproducts_(6619616945).jpg" title="放大"></a></div>Evenproduct的应急坑衬套件</div></div></div>
<h3><span id=".E5.BA.94.E6.80.A5.EF.BC.88Emergency.EF.BC.89.E5.8D.AB.E7.94.9F.E8.AE.BE.E6.96.BD"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="应急（Emergency）卫生设施">应急（Emergency）卫生设施</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%8D%AB%E7%94%9F%E8%AE%BE%E6%96%BD&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="编辑章节：应急（Emergency）卫生设施">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Emergency sanitation" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="应急卫生设施"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%BA%94%E6%80%A5%E5%8D%AB%E7%94%9F%E8%AE%BE%E6%96%BD&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="应急卫生设施（页面不存在）">应急卫生设施</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Emergency_sanitation" title="en:Emergency sanitation"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Emergency sanitation</span></a></span>）</span></span>在某些情况下是必需的，比如自然灾害，以及救济<a href="/wiki/%E9%9A%BE%E6%B0%91" title="难民">难民</a>和<a href="/wiki/%E5%9B%BD%E5%86%85%E6%B5%81%E7%A6%BB%E5%A4%B1%E6%89%80%E8%80%85" title="国内流离失所者">国内流离失所者</a>（IDP）。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Harveybook_20-0"><a href="#cite_note-Harveybook-20">[20]</a></sup>应急卫生设施有三种使用周期：即时的、短期的和长期的。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Harveybook_20-1"><a href="#cite_note-Harveybook-20">[20]</a></sup>对于即时的应急卫生设施，重点是管理<a href="/wiki/%E9%9C%B2%E5%A4%A9%E6%8E%92%E4%BE%BF" title="露天排便">露天排便</a>，而厕所技术可能会包含非常基本的<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Latrine" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="原始厕所"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%8E%9F%E5%A7%8B%E5%8E%95%E6%89%80&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="原始厕所（页面不存在）">原始厕所</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latrine" title="en:Latrine"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Latrine</span></a></span>）</span></span>、<a href="/wiki/%E6%97%B1%E5%BB%81" title="旱廁">旱厕</a>、<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Bucket toilet" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="桶式厕所"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%A1%B6%E5%BC%8F%E5%8E%95%E6%89%80&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="桶式厕所（页面不存在）">桶式厕所</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bucket_toilet" title="en:Bucket toilet"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Bucket toilet</span></a></span>）</span></span>、<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Container-based sanitation" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="基于容器的卫生设施"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9F%BA%E4%BA%8E%E5%AE%B9%E5%99%A8%E7%9A%84%E5%8D%AB%E7%94%9F%E8%AE%BE%E6%96%BD&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="基于容器的卫生设施（页面不存在）">基于容器的卫生设施</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Container-based_sanitation" title="en:Container-based sanitation"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Container-based sanitation</span></a></span>）</span></span>和<a href="/wiki/%E5%8C%96%E5%AD%B8%E5%BB%81%E6%89%80" title="化學廁所">化学厕所</a>。短期的应急卫生设施可能还会涉及<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Urine-diverting dry toilet" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="尿便分离旱厕"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%B0%BF%E4%BE%BF%E5%88%86%E7%A6%BB%E6%97%B1%E5%8E%95&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="尿便分离旱厕（页面不存在）">尿便分离旱厕</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Urine-diverting_dry_toilet" title="en:Urine-diverting dry toilet"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Urine-diverting dry toilet</span></a></span>）</span></span>、<a href="/wiki/%E5%8C%96%E7%B3%9E%E6%B1%A0" title="化糞池">化粪池</a>、<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Decentralized wastewater system" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="分散式废水系统"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%88%86%E6%95%A3%E5%BC%8F%E5%BA%9F%E6%B0%B4%E7%B3%BB%E7%BB%9F&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="分散式废水系统（页面不存在）">分散式废水系统</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Decentralized_wastewater_system" title="en:Decentralized wastewater system"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Decentralized wastewater system</span></a></span>）</span></span>等技术。提供<a href="/wiki/%E6%B4%97%E6%89%8B" title="洗手">洗手</a>设施和<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Fecal sludge management" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="粪便污泥管理"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%B2%AA%E4%BE%BF%E6%B1%A1%E6%B3%A5%E7%AE%A1%E7%90%86&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="粪便污泥管理（页面不存在）">粪便污泥管理</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fecal_sludge_management" title="en:Fecal sludge management"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Fecal sludge management</span></a></span>）</span></span>也是应急卫生设施的一部分。<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Sphere (organization)" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="领域组织"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%A2%86%E5%9F%9F%E7%BB%84%E7%BB%87&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="领域组织（页面不存在）">领域组织</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sphere_(organization)" title="en:Sphere (organization)"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Sphere (organization)</span></a></span>）</span></span>的手册为灾难或冲突之后的卫生设施提供了保护原则与核心标准。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E7.8E.AF.E5.A2.83.EF.BC.88Environmental.EF.BC.89.E5.8D.AB.E7.94.9F.E8.AE.BE.E6.96.BD"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="环境（Environmental）卫生设施">环境（Environmental）卫生设施</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%8D%AB%E7%94%9F%E8%AE%BE%E6%96%BD&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="编辑章节：环境（Environmental）卫生设施">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>环境卫生设施涵盖了对与疾病<a href="/wiki/%E4%BC%A0%E6%92%AD%E9%80%94%E5%BE%84" title="传播途径">传播途径</a>有关的环境因素的控制。这一类别下面包括固体废物管理、水和<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%BA%9F%E6%B0%B4" title="废水">废水</a>处理、<a href="/wiki/%E5%B7%A5%E6%A5%AD%E5%BB%A2%E6%96%99" title="工業廢料">工业废料</a>处理以及噪音和污染控制。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E6.94.B9.E5.96.84.E7.9A.84.E5.92.8C.E6.9C.AA.E6.94.B9.E5.96.84.E7.9A.84.EF.BC.88Improved_and_unimproved.EF.BC.89.E5.8D.AB.E7.94.9F.E8.AE.BE.E6.96.BD"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="改善的和未改善的（Improved_and_unimproved）卫生设施">改善的和未改善的（Improved and unimproved）卫生设施</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%8D%AB%E7%94%9F%E8%AE%BE%E6%96%BD&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="编辑章节：改善的和未改善的（Improved and unimproved）卫生设施">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Improved sanitation" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="改善的卫生设施"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%94%B9%E5%96%84%E7%9A%84%E5%8D%AB%E7%94%9F%E8%AE%BE%E6%96%BD&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="改善的卫生设施（页面不存在）">改善的卫生设施</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Improved_sanitation" title="en:Improved sanitation"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Improved sanitation</span></a></span>）</span></span>和未改善的卫生设施指的是家庭层面的人类粪便管理。该术语是<a href="/wiki/%E4%B8%96%E7%95%8C%E5%8D%AB%E7%94%9F%E7%BB%84%E7%BB%87" title="世界卫生组织">世界卫生组织</a>/<a href="/wiki/%E8%81%94%E5%90%88%E5%9B%BD%E5%84%BF%E7%AB%A5%E5%9F%BA%E9%87%91%E4%BC%9A" title="联合国儿童基金会">联合国儿童基金会</a>的<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Joint Monitoring Programme for Water Supply and Sanitation" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="供水与卫生设施联合监测计划"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%BE%9B%E6%B0%B4%E4%B8%8E%E5%8D%AB%E7%94%9F%E8%AE%BE%E6%96%BD%E8%81%94%E5%90%88%E7%9B%91%E6%B5%8B%E8%AE%A1%E5%88%92&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="供水与卫生设施联合监测计划（页面不存在）">供水与卫生设施联合监测计划</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Joint_Monitoring_Programme_for_Water_Supply_and_Sanitation" title="en:Joint Monitoring Programme for Water Supply and Sanitation"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Joint Monitoring Programme for Water Supply and Sanitation</span></a></span>）</span></span>用于描述<a href="/wiki/%E5%8D%83%E5%B9%B4%E5%8F%91%E5%B1%95%E7%9B%AE%E6%A0%87" title="千年发展目标">千年发展目标</a>在卫生设施方面的目标的指标。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E7.BC.BA.E4.B9.8F.EF.BC.88Lack_of.EF.BC.89.E5.8D.AB.E7.94.9F.E8.AE.BE.E6.96.BD"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="缺乏（Lack_of）卫生设施">缺乏（Lack of）卫生设施</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%8D%AB%E7%94%9F%E8%AE%BE%E6%96%BD&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="编辑章节：缺乏（Lack of）卫生设施">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>实际上，缺乏卫生设施通常意味着缺乏任何人都想自愿使用的厕所或卫生的厕所。缺乏卫生设施的结果通常是<a href="/wiki/%E9%9C%B2%E5%A4%A9%E6%8E%92%E4%BE%BF" title="露天排便">露天排便</a>（和露天排尿，但这是不太令人关心的）及其相关的严重公共健康问题。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-21"><a href="#cite_note-21">[21]</a></sup>据估计，截至2015年，仍有24亿人缺乏<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Improved sanitation" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="改善的卫生设施"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%94%B9%E5%96%84%E7%9A%84%E5%8D%AB%E7%94%9F%E8%AE%BE%E6%96%BD&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="改善的卫生设施（页面不存在）">改善的卫生设施</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Improved_sanitation" title="en:Improved sanitation"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Improved sanitation</span></a></span>）</span></span>，其中6.6亿人缺乏安全的饮用水。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-sanitation_22-0"><a href="#cite_note-sanitation-22">[22]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id=".E7.8E.B0.E5.9C.BA.EF.BC.88Onsite.EF.BC.89.E5.8D.AB.E7.94.9F.E8.AE.BE.E6.96.BD"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="现场（Onsite）卫生设施">现场（Onsite）卫生设施</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%8D%AB%E7%94%9F%E8%AE%BE%E6%96%BD&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="编辑章节：现场（Onsite）卫生设施">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>现场卫生设施被定义为“在粪便和废水产生的地点即对其进行收集、储存或处理的卫生设施系统”。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Tilley_13-2"><a href="#cite_note-Tilley-13">[13]</a></sup><sup class="reference" style="white-space:nowrap;">:173</sup>处理程度可能会有所不同，从不处理到先进处理。例如坑式<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Latrine" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="原始厕所"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%8E%9F%E5%A7%8B%E5%8E%95%E6%89%80&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="原始厕所（页面不存在）">原始厕所</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latrine" title="en:Latrine"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Latrine</span></a></span>）</span></span>（不处理）和<a href="/wiki/%E5%8C%96%E7%B3%9E%E6%B1%A0" title="化糞池">化粪池</a>（经<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%B1%A1%E6%B0%B4%E5%A4%84%E7%90%86" title="污水处理">污水处理</a>）。现场卫生设施系统经常会连接到<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Fecal sludge management" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="粪便污泥管理"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%B2%AA%E4%BE%BF%E6%B1%A1%E6%B3%A5%E7%AE%A1%E7%90%86&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="粪便污泥管理（页面不存在）">粪便污泥管理</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fecal_sludge_management" title="en:Fecal sludge management"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Fecal sludge management</span></a></span>）</span></span>系统，在现场产生的粪便污泥就能在异地处理。只有当建筑物内部或附近有管道<a href="/wiki/%E4%BE%9B%E6%B0%B4" title="供水">供水</a>时才会产生<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%BA%9F%E6%B0%B4" title="废水">废水</a>（污水）。
</p><p>一个相关的术语是<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Decentralized wastewater system" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="分散式废水系统"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%88%86%E6%95%A3%E5%BC%8F%E5%BA%9F%E6%B0%B4%E7%B3%BB%E7%BB%9F&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="分散式废水系统（页面不存在）">分散式废水系统</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Decentralized_wastewater_system" title="en:Decentralized wastewater system"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Decentralized wastewater system</span></a></span>）</span></span>，特别是指现场卫生设施的废水部分。同样，<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Onsite sewage facility" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="现场污水设施"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%8E%B0%E5%9C%BA%E6%B1%A1%E6%B0%B4%E8%AE%BE%E6%96%BD&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="现场污水设施（页面不存在）">现场污水设施</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Onsite_sewage_facility" title="en:Onsite sewage facility"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Onsite sewage facility</span></a></span>）</span></span>可以处理现场产生的废水。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E5.AE.89.E5.85.A8.E7.AE.A1.E7.90.86.E7.9A.84.EF.BC.88Safely_managed.EF.BC.89.E5.8D.AB.E7.94.9F.E8.AE.BE.E6.96.BD"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="安全管理的（Safely_managed）卫生设施">安全管理的（Safely managed）卫生设施</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%8D%AB%E7%94%9F%E8%AE%BE%E6%96%BD&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="编辑章节：安全管理的（Safely managed）卫生设施">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Joint Monitoring Programme for Water Supply and Sanitation" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="供水与卫生设施联合监测计划"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%BE%9B%E6%B0%B4%E4%B8%8E%E5%8D%AB%E7%94%9F%E8%AE%BE%E6%96%BD%E8%81%94%E5%90%88%E7%9B%91%E6%B5%8B%E8%AE%A1%E5%88%92&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="供水与卫生设施联合监测计划（页面不存在）">JMP</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Joint_Monitoring_Programme_for_Water_Supply_and_Sanitation" title="en:Joint Monitoring Programme for Water Supply and Sanitation"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Joint Monitoring Programme for Water Supply and Sanitation</span></a></span>）</span></span>定义现在将较高水平的卫生设施服务称为“安全管理的卫生设施”。这是基本的卫生设施服务，粪便可以安全地就地处置，也可以运输到异地处理。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-JMP2017_8-3"><a href="#cite_note-JMP2017-8">[8]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id=".E5.8F.AF.E6.8C.81.E7.BB.AD.EF.BC.88Sustainable.EF.BC.89.E5.8D.AB.E7.94.9F.E8.AE.BE.E6.96.BD"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="可持续（Sustainable）卫生设施">可持续（Sustainable）卫生设施</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%8D%AB%E7%94%9F%E8%AE%BE%E6%96%BD&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="编辑章节：可持续（Sustainable）卫生设施">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Sustainable sanitation" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="可持续卫生设施"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%8F%AF%E6%8C%81%E7%BB%AD%E5%8D%AB%E7%94%9F%E8%AE%BE%E6%96%BD&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="可持续卫生设施（页面不存在）">可持续卫生设施</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sustainable_sanitation" title="en:Sustainable sanitation"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Sustainable sanitation</span></a></span>）</span></span>考虑整个“卫生设施价值链”，包括用户的经验、<a href="/wiki/%E6%8E%92%E6%B3%84%E7%89%A9" title="排泄物">排泄物</a>和<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%BA%9F%E6%B0%B4" title="废水">废水</a>的收集方法、废物的运输、处理和再利用或处置。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Tilley_13-3"><a href="#cite_note-Tilley-13">[13]</a></sup>大约从2009年，该词被广泛使用。2007年，<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Sustainable Sanitation Alliance" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="可持续卫生设施联盟"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%8F%AF%E6%8C%81%E7%BB%AD%E5%8D%AB%E7%94%9F%E8%AE%BE%E6%96%BD%E8%81%94%E7%9B%9F&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="可持续卫生设施联盟（页面不存在）">可持续卫生设施联盟</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sustainable_Sanitation_Alliance" title="en:Sustainable Sanitation Alliance"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Sustainable Sanitation Alliance</span></a></span>）</span></span>定义了五项可持续性标准来比较卫生设施系统的可持续性。为了保持可持续性，卫生设施系统必须在经济上可行，在社会上可接受，在技术和体制上适当，并且还应该保护环境和自然资源。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-:2_2-1"><a href="#cite_note-:2-2">[2]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id=".E5.85.B6.E5.AE.83"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="其它">其它</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%8D%AB%E7%94%9F%E8%AE%BE%E6%96%BD&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="编辑章节：其它">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>用来描述某些类型卫生设施的其它术语包括： 
</p>
<ul><li>基于社区的卫生设施（通常与<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Decentralized wastewater system" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="分散式废水系统"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%88%86%E6%95%A3%E5%BC%8F%E5%BA%9F%E6%B0%B4%E7%B3%BB%E7%BB%9F&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="分散式废水系统（页面不存在）">分散式废水系统</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Decentralized_wastewater_system" title="en:Decentralized wastewater system"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Decentralized wastewater system</span></a></span>）</span></span>相关）</li></ul>
<h2><span id=".E5.81.A5.E5.BA.B7.E6.96.B9.E9.9D.A2"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="健康方面">健康方面</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%8D%AB%E7%94%9F%E8%AE%BE%E6%96%BD&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="编辑章节：健康方面">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:F-diagram-01.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2608" data-file-width="6600" decoding="async" height="87" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/99/F-diagram-01.jpg/220px-F-diagram-01.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/99/F-diagram-01.jpg/330px-F-diagram-01.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/99/F-diagram-01.jpg/440px-F-diagram-01.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:F-diagram-01.jpg" title="放大"></a></div>“F图”展示了<a href="/wiki/%E7%B2%AA%E5%8F%A3%E8%B7%AF%E5%BE%84" title="粪口路径">粪口疾病传播途径</a>。“F”代表几个以“F”开头的单词——<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%B2%AA%E4%BE%BF" title="粪便">Feces</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E6%89%8B%E6%8C%87" title="手指">Finger</a>、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%92%BC%E8%A0%85" title="蒼蠅">Fly</a>、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%94%B0%E5%9C%B0" title="田地">Field</a>、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%B0%B4%E4%BD%93" title="水体">Fluid</a>和<a href="/wiki/%E9%A3%9F%E7%89%A9" title="食物">Food</a>。蓝竖线表示切断传播途径的方式：<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%A9%AC%E6%A1%B6" title="马桶">马桶</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E4%BE%9B%E6%B0%B4" title="供水">安全饮水</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E5%8D%AB%E7%94%9F%E5%AD%A6" title="卫生学">卫生保健</a>及<a href="/wiki/%E6%B4%97%E6%89%8B" title="洗手">洗手</a>。</div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><video class="thumbimage" controls="" data-durationhint="120" data-mwprovider="wikimediacommons" data-mwtitle="Dalberg_Water_Week_Final.webm" height="124" id="mwe_player_1" poster="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/02/Dalberg_Water_Week_Final.webm/220px--Dalberg_Water_Week_Final.webm.jpg" preload="none" width="220"><source data-bandwidth="809000" data-framerate="24000.384" data-height="480" data-shorttitle="VP9 480P" data-title="标清VP9（480P）" data-transcodekey="480p.vp9.webm" data-width="854" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/transcoded/0/02/Dalberg_Water_Week_Final.webm/Dalberg_Water_Week_Final.webm.480p.vp9.webm" type='video/webm;
